Source Code

000001,000001:                                                                                                 #  Copyright:     Public domain.
000002,000002:                                                                                                 #  Filename:      MAIN.agc
000003,000003:                                                                                                 #  Purpose:       Part of the source code for Colossus, build 249.
000004,000004:                                                                                                 #                 It is part of the source code for the Command Module's (CM)
000005,000005:                                                                                                 #                 Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC), possibly for Apollo 8 and 9.
000006,000006:                                                                                                 #  Assembler:     yaYUL
000007,000007:                                                                                                 #  Contact:       Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
000008,000008:                                                                                                 #  Website:       www.ibiblio.org/apollo
000009,000009:                                                                                                 #  Mod history:   04/30/03 RSB.   Created using the Luminary131 file of the 
000010,000010:                                                                                                 #                                 same name as a model.
000011,000011:                                                                                                 #                 08/02/04 RSB    Resumed Colossus development.
000012,000012:                                                                                                 #                 08/22/04 RSB    Filled in all of the page numbers for the
000013,000013:                                                                                                 #                                 individual include-files.
000014,000014: 
000015,000015:                                                                                                 #  The contents of the "Colossus249" files, in general, are transcribed 
000016,000016:                                                                                                 #  from a scanned document obtained from MIT's website,
000017,000017:                                                                                                 #  http://hrst.mit.edu/hrs/apollo/public/archive/1701.pdf.  I'd like to note
000018,000018:                                                                                                 #  that the character-set of the line-printer used must not have completely
000019,000019:                                                                                                 #  agreed with the one the developers had in mind, so I've interpreted various
000020,000020:                                                                                                 #  wacky symbols appearing in the print as follows:
000021,000021: 
000022,000022:                                                                                                 #         Print                           Interpretation
000023,000023:                                                                                                 #         -----                           --------------
000024,000024:                                                                                                 #         plus-minus                            <
000025,000025:                                                                                                 #         lower-case Greek delta                >
000026,000026:                                                                                                 #         lower-case Greek nu              | (sometimes)
000027,000027:                                                                                                 #         strange lower-case d                  &
000028,000028:                                                                                                 #         trailing '                            :
000029,000029:                                                                                                 #         other                           still uninterpreted
000030,000030: 
000031,000031:                                                                                                 #  Notations on the scanned document read, in part:
000032,000032: 
000033,000033:                                                                                                 #         Assemble revision 249 of AGC program Colossus by NASA
000034,000034:                                                                                                 #         2021111-041.  October 28, 1968.  
000035,000035: 
000036,000036:                                                                                                 #         This AGC program shall also be referred to as
000037,000037:                                                                                                 #                                 Colossus 1A
000038,000038: 
000039,000039:                                                                                                 #         Prepared by
000040,000040:                                                                                                 #                         Massachussets Institute of Technology
000041,000041:                                                                                                 #                         75 Cambridge Parkway
000042,000042:                                                                                                 #                         Cambridge, Massachusetts
000043,000043:                                                                                                 #         under NASA contract NAS 9-4065.
000044,000044: 
000045,000045:                                                                                                 #  Refer directly to the online document mentioned above for further information.
000046,000046:                                                                                                 #  Please report any errors (relative to 1701.pdf) to info@sandroid.org.
000047,000047: 
000048,000048:                                                                                                 #  This file is a little different from the other Colossus249 files I'm providing, 
000049,000049:                                                                                                 #  in that it doesn't represent anything that appears directly in the original source.  
000050,000050:                                                                                                 #  What I (RSB) have done for organizational purposes is to split the huge monolithic
000051,000051:                                                                                                 #  source code into smaller, more manageable chunks--i.e., into individual source 
000052,000052:                                                                                                 #  files.  Those files are rejoined within this file as "includes".  It just makes
000053,000053:                                                                                                 #  it a little easier to work with.  The code chunks correspond to natural divisions
000054,000054:                                                                                                 #  into sub-programs.  In fact, these divisions are more-or-less specified by
000055,000055:                                                                                                 #  the source code itself.  Refer to the "SUBROUTINE CALLS" at the
000056,000056:                                                                                                 #  very beginning of the file ASSEMBLY_AND_OPERATION_INFORMATION.agc.
000057,000057: 
000058,000058:                                                                                                 #  It may be reasonably asked why tens of thousands of lines of source are joined by
000059,000059:                                                                                                 #  means of inclusion, rather than simply assembling the source files individually and
000060,000060:                                                                                                 #  then linking them to form the executable.  The answer is that the original 
000061,000061:                                                                                                 #  development team had no linker.  The builds were monolithic just like this.
000062,000062:                                                                                                 #  There was a big emphasis on reusability of the code in the original project, 
000063,000063:                                                                                                 #  apparently, but this reusability took the form of inserting your deck of 
000064,000064:                                                                                                 #  punch-cards at the appropriate position in somebody else's deck of punch-cards.
000065,000065:                                                                                                 #  So, indeed, the method of file-inclusion is a very fair representation of the 
000066,000066:                                                                                                 #  methods used in the original development ... with the improvement, of course,
000067,000067:                                                                                                 #  that you no longer have to worry about dropping the card deck.  On the other hand, 
000068,000068:                                                                                                 #  I wasn't there at the time, so I may have no idea what I'm talking about.
000069,000069: 
000070,000070:                                                                                                 #  Finally, note that the original Apollo AGC assembler (called "YUL") is no longer 
000071,000071:                                                                                                 #  available (as far as I can tell).  The replacement assembler yaYUL accepts 
000072,000072:                                                                                                 #  a slightly different format for the source code from what YUL accepted, so the 
000073,000073:                                                                                                 #  source code has been targeted for assembly with yaYUL.
000074,000074: 
000075,000075:                                                                                                 #  What follows is simply a bunch of file-includes for the individual code chunks.
000076,000076:                                                                                                 #  I've marked the page numbers vs. the original scanned listing (1701.pdf) to 
000077,000077:                                                                                                 #  make proof-reading easier.  Besides, the scanned listing contains a lot of
000078,000078:                                                                                                 #  interesting tables (cross-referenced to page numbers) created by YUL, 
000079,000079:                                                                                                 #  but not duplicated by yaYUL, so it's still valuable even if the source-files
000080,000080:                                                                                                 #  listed below are in hand.
000081,000081: 
000082,000082:                                                                                                 #  pp. 1-2 contain no code/comments.
